本科专业培养计划
Undergraduate Program for
Marine Electrical and Electronic Engineering Major
[2024级适用]
测控技术与仪器（080301）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
测控技术与仪器专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Measurement Control Technology and Instruments Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
本专业成立于2006年，并于2019年通过了教育部组织的全国工程教育专业认证，2020年被评为辽宁省一流本科教育示范专业。专业师资力量雄厚，职称年龄结构合理，大部分教师具有博士学位和工程经验，并承担有多项国家、省、部级科研课题，教师均具有较高的学术造诣和教育教学水平。本专业培养过程注重培养学生的创新实践能力，专业实验室拥有先进的实验设备。专业的培养质量获得社会第三方评价报告的肯定，多项指标名列前茅。
本专业是多学科复合型专业。培养学生德智体美劳全面发展、掌握电子技术、计算机技术、传感技术、信号处理技术、控制技术等交叉学科知识，具有信息检测与处理的综合应用能力、软件与硬件的协同设计能力和电子信息与仪器系统的研发创新能力的工程技术人才。
This major was established in 2006 and passed the national engineering education professional certification organized by the Ministry of education in 2019. In 2020, this major was rated as a first-class undergraduate education demonstration major in Liaoning Province. Teachers in this major have reasonable title and age structure, high academic attainments and teaching level. Most of the teachers have doctoral degrees and engineering practice experience, and undertake a number of national, provincial and ministerial scientific research projects. The training process of this major focuses on the cultivation of students' innovative practical ability. The professional laboratory has advanced experimental equipment. The quality of professional training has been affirmed by the third-party evaluation report of the society, and many indicators are among the best.
This major is a multi-disciplinary theory and technology of cross-disciplinary professional, which trains students to develop in an all-round way morally, intellectually, physically, aesthetically and laboriously. Besides, students are trained to master the interdisciplinary knowledge of electronic technology, computer technology, sensing technology, signal processing technology and control technology, so that they can have the comprehensive application ability of information detection and processing, the cooperative design ability of software and hardware, and the innovation ability of research and development of electronic information and instrument system.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业培养具备扎实的自然科学基础知识和测控技术与仪器专业知识，适应社会发展，能够从事智能仪器、电子信息系统、测控系统、港航仪器与系统相关的研究开发、工程设计、运行管理等工作，具有创新精神和国际视野，德智体美劳全面发展，能够成为社会主义合格建设者和可靠接班人的工程技术人才。
毕业生毕业五年左右能达到：
1、具有家国情怀与社会责任感，爱国敬业，身心健康，遵守法律法规、职业道德、行业标准和规范；
2、能够综合运用工程知识解决智能仪器、电子信息系统、测控系统、港航仪器与系统相关的复杂工程问题，并能综合考虑和评价工程对环境与社会各方面的影响；
3、能有效沟通和交流，在团队中发挥有效作用；
4、具有创新思维和国际视野，能够跟踪本领域新技术，能不断学习提高并适应社会发展。
This major cultivates qualified socialist builders and reliable successors of engineering and technical personnel. They have solid basic knowledge and professional knowledge of natural sciences, can adapt to social development. They are able to engage in research and development, design and operation management related to intelligent instruments, electronic information systems, measurement and control systems, and marine instrument systems. At the same time, they have the spirit of innovation and international vision, and can develop in an all-round way.
The students will achieve followings after they graduate five years:
1. Have family and country feelings and a sense of social responsibility, patriotism and dedication, physical and mental health, abide by laws and regulations, professional ethics, industry standards and norms.
2. Be able to comprehensively use engineering knowledge to solve complex engineering problems related to intelligent instruments, electronic information systems, measurement and control systems, marine instruments and systems, and to comprehensively consider and evaluate the impact of the project on the environment and society.
3. Be able to communicate effectively and play an effective role in the team.
4. Possess strong ability of innovation and international vision, be able to track new technologies and continuously learn to improve and adapt to social development.

USV sensing and control technology, Ship Automation System, Fundamentals of Marine Instruments, Port Logistics Automation Systems, Ship Practice (Engineering), Project Management Practice.

后    记
培养计划是高等学校人才培养的纲领性文件，是教育思想和办学理念的集中体现，是实现人才培养目标的具体实施方案。根据学校质量体系文件《培养计划的制定与修订》（DMU-2-040）的要求，培养计划原则上每4年修订一次，在特殊情况下可提前或推迟进行修订，我校培养计划上一次全面修订于2021年进行。为满足教育教学改革的需要，本年度培养计划在2023年修订版的基础上进行了再次修订。
本年度培养计划在多次校对、反复审核的过程当中，得到了各教学单位领导、教务、以及老师的大力支持和帮助。在此，对在培养计划修订过程中给予支持和帮助的各位，表示衷心的感谢。
培养计划的制定是一项繁琐的系统工作，难免会有疏漏，不足之处还望批评指正。培养计划的修订是以专业发展和知识更新为需求导向的，在执行过程中会进行细微调整。在此过程中，若产生分歧，应以教务系统为准。

电气工程及其自动化（080601）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
电气工程及其自动化专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Electrical Engineering and Automation Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
本专业为教育部高等学校特色专业建设点、辽宁省普通高等学校一流本科教育示范专业、辽宁省普通高等学校本科示范性专业、辽宁省普通高等学校本科重点支持专业、辽宁省普通高等学校本科综合改革试点专业。
本专业具有海洋工程特色明显、强电与弱电结合、理论与实践结合的特点。在专业培养计划中注重实践能力的培养，以适应社会对高质量工程技术人才的需要。本专业已成为辽宁省老工业基地改造，特别是辽宁船舶航运企业研发高附加值船舶电气技术等培养专门人才的重要高校基地。本专业师资力量强大，93%教师具有博士学位，正高级教师数量充足。
本专业拥有良好的实验教学设施设备，为学生提供优越的学习和发展条件，本专业实验中心被评为辽宁省电气工程实验教学示范中心。
Electrical engineering and automation major features the ministry of education featured program construction, as well as the first class undergraduate education demonstration major, the undergraduate demonstration major, the key support specialty and the undergraduate comprehensive reform pilot program of Liaoning province.
This major has obvious characteristics of marine engineering, combining strong and weak electricity, also theory and practice. In the training program, emphasis is laid on the cultivation of practical ability to meet the needs of society for high-quality engineering and technical personnel. This major has become an important university base for the reconstruction of old industrial bases in Liaoning province, especially Training professionals for the research and development of high value-added ship electrical technology in Liaoning shipping enterprises. The faculty of this major is strong, 93% of the teachers have doctoral degrees, and the number of senior teachers is sufficient.
This major has good experimental teaching facilities and equipment to provide students with superior learning and development conditions. The experimental center of this major was rated as the electrical engineering experimental teaching demonstration center of Liaoning province.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业坚持立德树人教育根本任务，培养适应社会主义现代化建设，服务于船舶、港口及其它领域现场电气工程师，能够从事与电气工程有关的系统运行、自动控制、信息处理、试验分析、研制开发、经济管理以及计算机技术应用等领域工作的“宽口径、复合型”德智体美劳全面发展的高级工程技术人才。
This major adheres to the fundamental task of promoting morality and cultivating people, and  trains the high-quality engineering talents adapting for the socialist modernization construction; serving for the ships, ports and other fields; being able to engage in the fields of electrical engineering and automation, such as system operation, automation, information processing, experimental analysis, development research, economic management, computer technology application.

Marine Power Station and Automatic Control Systems, Port Power System, Electrical Control Systems for Marine Machinery, High Voltage Technique, Electric Technology, Design and Practice of Electrical Motor, Design and Practice of Electrical Specialty Subject, Modeling and Simulation of Electrical Systems, Course Design and Practice of Power Electronics, Development and Design of Embedded System, Ship Observation Practice

大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
自动化专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Automation Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
自动化专业主要研究自动控制的原理和方法、自动化单元技术和集成技术及其在各类控制系统中的应用。它以自动控制理论为基础，以信息电子技术、电力电子技术、传感器技术、计算机技术、网络与通信技术为主要工具，面向工业生产过程自动控制及各行业、各部门的自动化。它具有“控（制）管（理）一体，强（电）弱（电）结合，软（件）硬（件）兼施”等鲜明的特点，是理、工、文、管多学科交叉的宽口径工科专业。本专业学生毕业后能够在国民经济、国防建设及社会发展多行业领域从事自动控制系统设计、运行管理及新技术研发等工作，尤其是还可以满足港航企事业单位对于控制领域专门人才的需求，并为高等院校、科研院所输送高一级后备人才。
Automation major mainly studies the principle and method of Automatic Control, Automatic Unit Technology and Integration Technology and their applications in various control systems. It is based on the Automatic Control Theory with the application of Information Electronics Technology，Power Electronic Technology , Sensor Technology, Computer Technology, Network and Communication Technology as the primary tools. This major provides the training necessary for automation control in the process of industrial production in various industries and different divisions. Automation major integrates the control and management, combines strong electricity and weak electricity, and performs both the software and hardware. With the emphasis of such distinctive characteristics, this major covers cross-disciplinary knowledge of science, engineering, arts and management. Graduates of Automatic Control Technology program have found employment in industries of national economy, the Building of National Defense, and multi social developing industries, undertaking Automatic Control System design, operational management and technological research and development. In particular, they meet Shipping Enterprises’ demand of talents in control field. Many of the graduates also devote to educational researches in institutions of higher learning and the Scientific Research Institute as outstanding reserve personnel.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业主要以船舶航运及海洋工程为背景，培养在控制科学与自动化工程技术领域从事研究开发、工程设计、运行管理等工作的复合型工程技术人才。
本专业学生毕业后，经过5年左右实际工作锻炼，将达成以下目标：
1. 具有人文与社会科学素养、社会责任感、职业道德和工程伦理，遵守法律法规、行业标准和规范；
2. 能够综合运用数理、工程和专业知识，为相关自动化领域复杂工程问题提供全面的解决方案和系统设计；
3. 具备良好的沟通、交流与管理能力，能在团队中发挥有效作用；
4. 具有全球化视野，洞悉相关领域自动化系统的发展动态和前沿技术，具有终身学习和一定的创新能力，以适应社会发展。
This major mainly takes ship shipping and marine engineering as the background, and cultivates composite engineering and technical talents engaged in research and development, engineering design, operation management and other work in the field of control science and automation engineering technology.
Our graduates from this program, after about five years of practical works, will achieve following objectives:
1. Hold humanities and social science literacy, social responsibility, professional ethics and engineering ethics, comply with laws and regulations, industry standards and norms.
2. Ability to use a combination of mathematical, engineering and professional knowledge to provide comprehensive solutions and system design for complex engineering problems in the relevant automation field.
3. Possess good communication and management skills, and can play an effective role in the team.
4. With a global perspective, insight into the development dynamics and cutting-edge technologies of automation systems in related fields, possess lifelong learning and certain innovative capabilities to adapt to social development.
三、毕业要求
III．Graduation Requirements

船舶运动控制、船舶自动化系统、船舶电力控制系统、船舶机舱控制系统、港口物流自动化系统、航海仪器基础。
Ship Maneuver Control, Ship Automation System, Ship Electric Power Control System，Ship Engine Room Control System，Port Logistics Automation Systems，Fundamentals of Marine Instrument.

毕业要求1 Requirement 1	工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学知识、工程基础用于解决智能仪器、电子信息系统、测控系统、港航仪器与系统相关的复杂工程问题。 Engineering Knowledge: Be able to use mathematics, natural science knowledge, and engineering foundations to solve complex engineering problems related to intelligent instruments, electronic information systems, measurement and control systems, and marine instruments and systems.
毕业要求2 Requirement 2	问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，对智能仪器、电子信息系统、测控系统、港航仪器与系统相关的复杂工程问题进行识别、表达，并通过文献，研究分析复杂工程问题，以获得有效结论。 Problem Analyzing: Be able to apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural sciences and engineering sciences to identify and express complex engineering problems related to intelligent instruments, electronic information systems, measurement and control systems, marine instruments and systems. Through literature, research and analysis of complex engineering issues to obtain effective conclusions.
毕业要求3 Requirement 3	设计 / 开发解决方案：能够针对智能仪器、电子信息系统、测控系统、港航仪器与系统相关的复杂工程问题，设计满足要求的检测和处理单元、数据处理及控制算法、测量仪器或系统，或者能够选择合适的测量控制单元、系统设备及软件，提出解决方案，能够在设计或开发的过程体现创新意识并考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化及环境因素。 Designation/Development of Solutions: It is capable of designing detection and processing units, data processing and control algorithms, measuring instruments or systems that meet the requirements for complex engineering problems related to intelligent instruments, electronic information systems, measurement and control systems, marine instruments and systems. Be able to select the appropriate measurement control unit, system equipment and software, and propose solutions. Be able to reflect the sense of innovation in the design or development process and consider social, health, safety, legal, cultural and environmental factors.
毕业要求4 Requirement 4	研究：能够利用系统分析、建模、仿真、测试的基本理论和方法，对智能仪器、电子信息系统、测控系统、港航仪器与系统相关的复杂工程问题进行研究，针对问题设计测试试验方案，并综合研究结果和试验数据等信息给出正确的分析结论。 Research: Be able to use the basic theories and methods of system analysis, modeling, simulation, and testing to study complex engineering issues related to intelligent instruments, electronic information systems, measurement and control systems, and marine instruments and systems. According to the problem, the test plan is designed, and the information such as the research results and the test data is integrated to give the correct analysis conclusion.
毕业要求5 Requirement 5	使用现代工具：能够针对智能仪器、电子信息系统、测控系统、港航仪器与系统相关的复杂工程问题，开发或选择适当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，使用有效的方法进行仿真和模拟分析并能够理解其适用范围。 Using Modern Tools: Be able to develop or select appropriate technologies, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology tools for complex engineering problems related to Intelligent instruments, electronic information systems, measurement and control systems, marine instruments and systems. Use effective methods for simulation and simulation analysis and be able to understand its scope of application.
毕业要求6 Requirement 6	工程与社会：了解与本专业相关行业领域的生产和应用过程中涉及的政策、法律和法规，分析和评价其生产与应用过程对社会、健康、安全、法律及文化等因素的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 Engineering and Society: Understand the policies, laws and regulations involved in the production and application process of the industry related to this major. Analyze and evaluate the impact of its production and application processes on social, health, safety, legal and cultural factors, and understand the responsibilities that should be undertaken.
毕业要求7 Requirement 7	环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价智能仪器、电子信息系统、测控系统、港航仪器与系统等工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 Environment and Sustainable Development: Be able to understand and evaluate the impact of engineering practices such as intelligent instruments, electronic information systems, measurement and control systems, marine instruments and systems on the environment and sustainable development of society.
毕业要求8 Requirement 8	职业规范：具有良好的人文社会科学素养和社会责任感，能够在智能仪器、电子信息系统、测控系统、港航仪器与系统的设计和工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 Professional Norm: Possess good humanities and social science literacy and a sense of social responsibility. Be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms, and perform responsibilities in the design and engineering practice of intelligent instruments, electronic information systems, measurement and control systems, marine instruments and systems.
毕业要求9 Requirement 9	个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 Individuality and Team: Be able to undertake as an individual, a team member or a leader in a team with a multidisciplinary background.
毕业要求10 Requirement 10	沟通：能够就智能仪器、电子信息系统、测控系统、港航仪器与系统的工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行书面和口头的有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 Communication: Be able to communicate and communicate effectively with industry colleagues and the public on engineering issues of intelligent instruments, electronic information systems, measurement and control systems, marine instruments and systems, including writing reports and design manuscripts, presentations, clear expressions or responses instruction. Have a certain international perspective, and be able to communicate and communicate in a cross-cultural context.
毕业要求11 Requirement 11	项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 Project Management: Understand and master the principle of engineering management and the method of economic decision, and be able to use them in various field.
毕业要求12 Requirement 12	终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 Lifetime Study: Have the ability of continuous learning and adapt the development of the measurement & control technology and instrumentation. Have a correct understanding of the lifetime study.

1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.    2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. For details, please refer to the regulations on student status management in the student handbook.	1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.    2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. [Table 7]
毕业要求1 Graduation requirement 1	能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础及电气工程专业知识用于解决电气工程领域的复杂工程问题。 Be able to use mathematics, natural science, basic engineering and professional knowledge of electrical engineering to solve complex engineering problems in the field of electrical engineering.
毕业要求2 Graduation requirement 2	能够应用数学、自然科学和电气工程原理和方法，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析电气工程领域相关的复杂问题，以获得有效结论。 Be able to use mathematics, natural science and electrical engineering principles and methods to identify, express, and analyze the complex issues related to electrical engineering through the literature, in order to obtain effective conclusions.
毕业要求3 Graduation requirement 3	能够设计针对电气工程领域的复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、单元（部件）或工艺流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。 Be able to design a solution to resolve complex electrical engineering problems. The design of systems, units, or processes that meet specific requirements, and can reflect the sense of innovation in the design process, considering the social, health and safety, legal, cultural and environmental factors.
毕业要求4 Graduation requirement 4	能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对电气工程领域相关的复杂工程问题进行研究，包括设计与实验、分析与解释数据，并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 Be able to study the complex engineering problems related to electrical engineering field based on scientific principle and scientific methods, including system design and experiment, analysis and interpretation of data, and get the rational conclusion through comprehensive information.
毕业要求5 Graduation requirement 5	能够针对电气工程相关领域的复杂问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，对其进行预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。 Be able to develop, select and use appropriate technology, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology tools to predict and simulate the complicated problem of electrical engineering, and understand their limitations.
毕业要求6 Graduation requirement 6	能够基于工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价电气工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 Based on engineering background knowledge, be able to make reasonable analysis and evaluate the impact of electrical engineering practices and complex engineering problem solving on social, health, safety, law and culture, and understand the responsibilities.
毕业要求7 Graduation requirement 7	能够理解和评价针对复杂电气工程领域问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 Be able to understand and evaluate the impact of engineering practices for the complex issues in the field of electrical engineering onthe environmental and social sustainability.
毕业要求8 Graduation requirement 8	具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在工程实践中理解并遵守电气工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 Having the humanities and Social Sciences, social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by the professional ethics and norms of electrical engineering practice, to fulfill their responsibilities.
毕业要求9 Graduation requirement 9	能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 Be able to take on the role of individual, team members and leaders in a multidisciplinary team.
毕业要求10 Graduation requirement 10	能够就电气工程领域的复杂问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 Be able to communicate effectively with industry peers and the public for the complex problems in the field of electrical engineering, including report writing and presentation design, statement, commands express or respond. With an international perspective and be able to communicate and exchange ideas under the condition of diverse cultures.
毕业要求11 Graduation requirement 11	理解并掌握电气工程领域中工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 Understanding and mastering the principles of engineering management and the methods of economic decision and applying them in multiple disciplines.
毕业要求12 Graduation requirement 12	具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应社会经济发展的能力。 Having the awareness of independent learning and lifelong learning, and having the ability to learn continuously and adapt the development of social and economic.

1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.    2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. 毕业要求1 Requirement  1	工程知识：具有从事自动化工程所需的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识，并能够综合应用这些知识解决自动化领域复杂工程问题。 Engineering knowledge: Possess the knowledge that is required in automation engineering field, including mathematics, natural sciences, engineering foundation and professional expertise. Moreover, be able to use relevant knowledge to solve complex engineering problems in automation and related fields.
毕业要求2 Requirement  2	问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，对自动化领域的复杂工程问题进行识别、表达，并通过文献研究分析复杂工程问题，以获得有效结论。 Problem Analysis: Be able to apply the basic principle, recognition and expression of mathematics, natural sciences and engineering science, in addition to solve complex engineering problems in the field of automation through literature research, to obtain effective conclusions
毕业要求3 Requirement  3	设计/开发解决方案：能够针对自动化领域复杂工程问题，设计解决方案，设计满足需求的系统、单元或模块，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。并设计开发满足特定需求的控制系统、控制部件和控制流程。能够在设计环节中体现创新意识并考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化及环境等因素。 Solution Designs / developments: Aiming at the complex engineering problems in the field of automation, students are able to develop solutions and design the control system, unit or modules in the specific needs. Be able to embody innovative awareness in design process and consider social, health, safety, legal, cultural and environmental factors.
毕业要求4 Requirement  4	研究：能够基于科学原理对自动化领域的复杂工程问题进行研究，采用科学方法设计实验方案、分析与解释数据，并综合相关信息给出合理有效的结论。 Research：It is possible to study complex engineering problems in the field of automation based on scientific principles, design experimental schemes, analyze and interpret data using scientific methods, and provide relevant and reasonable information to give reasonable and effective conclusions.
毕业要求5 Requirement 5	使用现代工具：能够针对自动化领域的复杂工程问题，开发、选择与使用控制系统设计与仿真、计算机工程制图、电子电路设计与仿真等工具，包括对复杂工程问题的模拟与预测，并能够理解其局限性。 The Usage of Modern Tools: Be able to develop, select and use the design and simulation tools of control system, computer engineering drafting tools, design and simulation tools of electronic circuit for complex engineering problems in the automation field, including simulation and prediction of complex engineering problems, and to understand its limitations.
毕业要求6 Requirement  6	工程与社会：能够基于自动化工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价专业工程实践和自动化领域复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 Engineering and Social Responsibility: Be able to analyze reasonably based on automation engineering related background knowledge. Evaluate the effects of professional engineering practice and complex engineering solutions in the automation field to society, health, safety, law, and culture; understand and undertake the responsibility.
毕业要求7 Requirement  7	环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对自动化领域复杂工程问题的专业工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 Environment and Sustainable Development: Be able to understand and evaluate the impact of professional engineering practices on the environmental and social sustainability of complex engineering problems in the field of automation.
毕业要求8 Requirement  8	职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在自动化工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 Code of Ethics：Possess the humanities sciences and social sciences accomplishment and social responsibility. Be able to understand and obey the automation engineering practice in engineering ethics and norms, fulfilling the obligations.
毕业要求9 Requirement  9	个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 Individuality and Team: Be able to take on the role of individuality, team members and leaders in a multidisciplinary team.
毕业要求10 Requirement 10	沟通：能够就自动化领域复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文档、陈述发言、情绪表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。 Communication: Possess the ability to communicate effectively within the industry and the public on complex engineering problems in the field of automation, including writing reports and design documents, presentations, emotional expressions or response instructions. Possess a certain international perspective and the cross-cultural communication skill.
毕业要求11 Requirement 11	项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 Project Management: Understand and master the principles of engineering management and economic decision-making. Be able to apply in the knowledge in multidisciplinary environments.
毕业要求12 Requirement 12	终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 Lifelong learning: Possess the independent learning and lifelong learning awareness with the ability to learn and adapt to different environments.

1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.    2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. For details, please refer to the regulations on student status management in the student handbook.	1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.    2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits.
